  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_92261eab-7cd9-4a87-9b94-267f95cbbc7f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer3602722012951956109">In GATHERING DARKNESS, book three of the New York Times bestselling Falling Kingdoms series, the stakes have never been higher as three teams push forward on a race to find the Kindred, the four elemental crystals possessing ancient all-powerful magic, first:<br/><br/>Prince Magnus has just witnessed torture, death, and miracles during the bloody confrontation that decimated the reb</span>
  <span id="freeText3602722012951956109" style="display:none">In GATHERING DARKNESS, book three of the New York Times bestselling Falling Kingdoms series, the stakes have never been higher as three teams push forward on a race to find the Kindred, the four elemental crystals possessing ancient all-powerful magic, first:<br /><br />Prince Magnus has just witnessed torture, death, and miracles during the bloody confrontation that decimated the rebel forces. Now he must choose between family and justice as his father, the cruel King Gaius, sets out to conquer all of Mytica. All Gaius needs now are the Kindred - the four elemental crystals that give godlike powers to their owner. But the King of Blood is not the only one hunting for this ancient, storied magic...<br /><br />• THE KRAESHIANS join the hunt. Ashur and Amara, the royal siblings from the wealthy kingdom across the Silver Sea, charm and manipulate their way to the Kindred, proving to be more ruthless than perhaps even the King of Blood himself.<br /><br />• THE REBELS forge ahead. Princess Cleo and vengeful Jonas lead them, slaying with sweetness, skill, and a secret that can control Lucia's overpowering magic - all so they can use the Kindred to win back their fallen kingdoms.<br /><br />• THE WATCHERS follow Melenia out of the Sanctuary. They ally in the flesh with King Gaius, who vows to use Lucia's powers to unveil the Kindred.<br /><br />The only certainty in the dark times is that whoever finds the magic first will control the fate of Mytica... but fate can be fickle when magic is involved.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6317986454403032126"><b>DNF @ 28%</b><br/><br/>So here is the fucking deal.<br/><br/>I have <i>suffered</i> & I do mean <i>REALLY SUFFERED</i> with this series. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>I cannot deal with these paper-fucking-thin, shallow-ass, completely-not-even-worth-my-time, dumb-as-fucking-dirt characters.</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>I cannot deal with this boring-as-hell, killing-off-characters-left-and-right-for-shock-value, completely-derivative-of-every-fantasy-book-ever plot.</i>

  <span id="freeText6317986454403032126" style="display:none"><b>DNF @ 28%</b><br /><br />So here is the fucking deal.<br /><br />I have <i>suffered</i> &amp; I do mean <i>REALLY SUFFERED</i> with this series. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>I cannot deal with these paper-fucking-thin, shallow-ass, completely-not-even-worth-my-time, dumb-as-fucking-dirt characters.</i>

  <i>I cannot deal with this childish, who-even-edited-this, are-we-sure-someone-actually-fucking-edited-this writing.</i>
</b><br /><br />I don't even have the vocabulary to express how much I despise this series. <br /><br />Regardless of how much I didn't enjoy these books, I had <b>the best</b> time reading this with my lovely pals:<br /><br />♥ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/61971658-frankie-lovely" rel="nofollow noopener">Frankie</a><br />♥ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/47627265" rel="nofollow noopener">Kaylin</a><br />♥ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26462337" rel="nofollow noopener">Rachelle</a><br />♥ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17441031" rel="nofollow noopener">Jeremy</a><br />♥ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7971097" rel="nofollow noopener">Bentley</a><br /><br />But this is the end of the road for me. <div id="review_1931806774" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1931806774" />
    <a title="Bentley ★ Bookbastion.net" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7971097-bentley-bookbastion-net"><img alt="Bentley ★ Bookbastion.net" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589390032p2/7971097.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1931806774?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bentley ★ Bookbastion.net" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bentley ★ Bookbastion.net" href="/user/show/7971097-bentley-bookbastion-net">Bentley ★ Bookbastion.net</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7971097-bentley-bookbastion-net?shelf=wtf-did-i-just-read">wtf-did-i-just-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1931806774" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16977124010966587954"><i>See this review and more like it on <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.bookbastion.net'>www.bookbastion.net</a>!</i><br/>__________<br/><br/>Break out the bubbly for me friends, because I have finally <s>escaped</s> finished, this <s>pure torture</s> book! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388463343ra/7841127.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503098469ra/23628644.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503098560ra/23628650.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Cut to me, wondering where all the glowing reviews for this series come from, because I just don't get it. </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392745787ra/8604459.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>There are so many better written YA series out there</b> that I would recommend over this one, because this one's got problems. It's derivative to an extreme. Every plot point and character outline is lifted directly from Game of</span>
  <span id="freeText16977124010966587954" style="display:none"><i>See this review and more like it on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookbastion.net">www.bookbastion.net</a>!</i><br>__________<br><br>Break out the bubbly for me friends, because I have finally <s>escaped</s> finished, this <s>pure torture</s> book! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388463343ra/7841127.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503098469ra/23628644.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503098560ra/23628650.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Cut to me, wondering where all the glowing reviews for this series come from, because I just don't get it. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392745787ra/8604459.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>There are so many better written YA series out there</b> that I would recommend over this one, because this one's got problems. It's derivative to an extreme. Every plot point and character outline is lifted directly from Game of Thrones. You've got incestual siblings and their mean old dad who runs the world. You've got the downtrodden Stark daughter who has been separated from her family; and you've got the pure hearted do-gooders rebelling against those in power. <br><br>In this book, everything is painfully simplified. <b>There is no nuance to Morgan Rhode's writing.</b> When she wants you to know that a character's a bad dude, it's going to be telegraphed 14 times in earlier chapters before the big reveal so that there's absolutely no surprise. When she wants you to sympathize with a character she's going to give that character a stock scene where they pour their heart out in an overly sappy monologue that fairly screams: <i>"love him,"</i> which only made me dislike them even more. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503101693ra/23628933.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>It feels like there's no heart or soul to this series. No moral lessons underpinning the plot to make this series worth reading.</b> It's poorly plotted events and poorly drawn characters randomly bumping into each other over and over again and sometimes killing each other, which might be entertaining if it was well written. Spoiler alert: it's not, so it was painful to read. And not just for me either. <br><br>The Fantasy League I was reading this series with fell apart trying to get through this book. It wasn't from lack of trying - but rather a lack of a reason to care. This series killed off all our interest one by one like some horror movie slasher. By the time I finished it was like I'd just crawled out of the woods at the end of the movie, and I didn't even get an "I survived" t-shirt to make it worth it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503102220ra/23628996.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>I have to rant about the LGBT rep in this series.</b> In my review for Rebel Spring, I brought up some issues with a particular male character who was revealed to be bisexual. For the record, it was not the fact that this character was revealed to be bisexual that annoyed me. It was the way the reveal was treated: shoehorned into the final 30 pages of the story and the way it played out read more like sexual assault of an intoxicated character, rather than a romantic reveal.<br><br>Regardless, because Rhodes had already committed to the storyline at the end of the last book, I went into this one looking forward to seeing how it played out. It's more than disappointing. <br><br><b>It's badly handled and almost offensive to me as a gay man, because it's pretty clear Rhodes had no intention of showcasing a M/M romance in the same way she does her straight pairings. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503103165ra/23629070.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Keep in mind, at this point in the series Cleo has kissed every leading male character, including some of the ones that are now dead. <b>Straight characters hook up left, right and center in this series while the M/M relationship stagnates</b> and the characters dance around each other, never saying what they mean or expressing real romantic feelings for one another. <br><br><b>Frankly, It's not even a M/M relationship. It's a subplot that was shoehorned in for diversity rep by an author who clearly had no intentions of showcasing it in the same way as she does her straight relationships.</b> It's like someone told Morgan Rhodes that LGBT rep was profitable in the YA community and included the storyline only to draw in those readers, with no real intention to ever do anything with it. To drive that point home, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[she kills off one of the two involved in the relationship at the end of the book before their true feelings are ever discussed. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Seek out other books if you're looking for a well-written LGBT romance.</b> There are plenty of other YA books out there where the author actually wants to write those relationship dynamics. Really, I don't know why I expected more. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503104128ra/23629131.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Reaching the end of this review, I can feel the weight lifting right off my shoulders because I an finally done with this book, and this series. I won't be reading the rest because I couldn't care less what happens next. To be quite honest, I'll likely be avoiding Morgan Rhodes books in general in the future. <br><br><b>There's lots of great YA series out there. Give one of those a shot before spending money on this one.</b><br><br><b>★ = 1/5 stars, because Goodreads won't let me give less. </b><br><br>___________<br><blockquote>Buddy reading this hot mess with the Falling Kingdoms Fantasy League: <br><br>🗡<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/61971658-frankie-lovely" rel="nofollow noopener">Frankie Lovely</a><br>🗡<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">Mary, ~Ravager of Tomes~</a><br>🗡<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/47627265-kaylin" rel="nofollow noopener">Kaylin</a><br>🗡<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26462337-rachelle" rel="nofollow noopener">Rachelle</a><br>🗡<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17441031-jeremy" rel="nofollow noopener">Jeremy</a>
</blockquote><br><br>Lord, give me strength! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499573730ra/23246108.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16977124010966587954" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer655936550" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17167434135209792264">Q & A with Morgan Rhodes and you could win the whole Falling Kingdoms series, postcard set and a tshirt in <a href='http://youngadulthollywood.com/books/yah-interview-morgan-rhodes-talks-gathering-darkness-giveaway/#.VHzbCjHF-So' rel='nofollow noopener'>Young Adult Hollywood.</a><br/><br/><i>Wait a second.</i> I need to calm the rapid thumping in my chest. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405638544ra/10429162.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Okay. </b><br/><br/>Here we go.<br/><br/>Falling Kingdoms is one of my favorite series and its sequel Rebel Spring is by far my favorite book for so many reasons. It cemented my love for this series. And here comes the Gathering Darkness, this book is without mercy the most goriest<br/><br/>It is cruel and there would be a princess, a rebel </span>
  <span id="freeText17167434135209792264" style="display:none">Q &amp; A with Morgan Rhodes and you could win the whole Falling Kingdoms series, postcard set and a tshirt in <a href="http://youngadulthollywood.com/books/yah-interview-morgan-rhodes-talks-gathering-darkness-giveaway/#.VHzbCjHF-So" rel="nofollow noopener">Young Adult Hollywood.</a><br><br><i>Wait a second.</i> I need to calm the rapid thumping in my chest. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405638544ra/10429162.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Okay. </b><br><br>Here we go.<br><br>Falling Kingdoms is one of my favorite series and its sequel Rebel Spring is by far my favorite book for so many reasons. It cemented my love for this series. And here comes the Gathering Darkness, this book is without mercy the most goriest<br><br>It is cruel and there would be a princess, a rebel and a prince kissing but they don’t live happily ever after. They are still at <strong>
  <em>war. </em>
</strong><br><br>I wouldn’t highlight the book closely, in fear of spoiling the whole book to our dear readers and my friends. I’ll be <em>very </em>vague as I could be.<br><br>Gathering Darkness quickly follow up where Rebel Spring wrapped up. In this third book, everything escalated so fast, there was a whirlwind of disaster, romance and action. It was relatively easy to get lost into Rhodes's luscious but brutal world.<br><br><strong>Our main characters are back and they are sassier and baddest than yesterday.</strong> Every one of them is craftily written and layered as expected from Rhodes. There is nothing more interesting than seeing all of the main characters together having a fiery banter so I hope that would happen in the next couple of books.<br><br><strong>The romance doesn’t take over the plot, it is not the entire focus of the story. </strong>I don’t know if that’s a good thing or bad thing for some of the readers, but all I could say is I want more kissing. <strong>I definitely vote for more.</strong><br><br>The plot is intricate and there are so many twists every chapter. It is not a perfect book, I have a one problem with it, but aside from that Morgan Rhodes outdid herself again. AND THAT ENDING. <strong>Spoiler. </strong>It does not end well.<br><br>Gathering Darkness is such a great addition to the intense and magical series that is Falling Kingdoms. I am eager to see how the next couple of books would play out.<br><br>Review also posted at <a>Young Adult Hollywood.</a><br><br><i>Thanks to Morgan Rhodes for the ARC!</i><br><br><b>Edited September 20, 2014.</b><br><br>Cleo and Magnus have more sexual tension than I can actually deal with. THEY NEED TO HIT IT OFF AND STAY MARRIED FOREVER. <i>IM SORRY JONAS. </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392614815ra/8584505.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17167434135209792264" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1137398220" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1137398220" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1137398220?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1137398220" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15604052310059258250"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Believe in magic.Believe in the impossible.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I do believe in <b>magic</b>.I do believe in the <b>impossible</b>.I believe in acts of courage and kindness even when is seems a lost cause,I believe in the knight in shining armor (whoever that legendary rescuer might be,even myself),I believe that no matter what the good will prevail,and thanks to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17342700.Gathering_Darkness__Falling_Kingdoms___3_' title='Gathering Darkness (Falling Kingdoms, #3) by Morgan Rhodes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Gathering Darkness</a>,<b>I believe that even the most hideous actions,the most desperate and lost heroes can be redeemed</b>.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When the sorceress' blood is sp</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15604052310059258250" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Believe in magic.Believe in the impossible.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I do believe in <b>magic</b>.I do believe in the <b>impossible</b>.I believe in acts of courage and kindness even when is seems a lost cause,I believe in the knight in shining armor (whoever that legendary rescuer might be,even myself),I believe that no matter what the good will prevail,and thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17342700.Gathering_Darkness__Falling_Kingdoms___3_" title="Gathering Darkness (Falling Kingdoms, #3) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Gathering Darkness</a>,<b>I believe that even the most hideous actions,the most desperate and lost heroes can be redeemed</b>.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When the sorceress' blood is spilled,they will finally rise.And the world will burn.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The world will burn leaving nothing but ashes,but no one is willing to stop searching for the elemental crystals.As we learn more about the godesses and the reasons behind Melenia's interest in the world of the Mortals,Magnus is trying to deal with the devastated truths that were revealed to him,Cleo to reclaim her kingdom,Jonas to keep the resistance alive and Lucia to fight the gathering darkness that tries to consume her.The Kraeshian royals seem determined to find the Kindred for themselves,the Watchers are divided and the people of Mytica still suffer under the cruel rule of the King of Blood.<i>Blood is the answer to everything.</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Hatred is like fire.It burns the one who harnesses it.It's also extremely hard to see more helpful truths through its flames.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Even though the third book of the <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> series started off rather slowly,it truly compensated in the last chapters.I could hear my heart pounding loudly in my chest,my jaw was clenched and I tried really hard to deal with the <b>numerous deaths</b> and <b>revelations</b> and the choices some of the heroes made.<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5295120.Morgan_Rhodes" title="Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Morgan Rhodes</a> can cause some strong emotions and make her heroes become a part of your universe,to make you concerned about them and their future,and share their feelings.There were many interesting characters (and most of them died,obviously) and she effortlessly prepared the road for an intense next book (until the release of which I will suffer,again obviously.)<br><blockquote>
<b><i>“Some sought revenge against their mortal enemies with the edge of a sword. Her plan for vengeance began with the edge of a smile.</i></b>”</blockquote><br>Cleo is developing her deception skills,she tries to manipulate and guide people towards her goal,despite the ache in her heart every time she has to pretend that she has made peace with the demise of her family and the loss of her kingdom.I still fiercely believe that her cause is the right one and that her heart is the purest,she actually came to care about Lucia and she fought to discover something good in Magnus.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448445377ra/17141860.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There is no goodness inside of me princess,so please don't waste time fantasizing that there might be.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But <i>there is</i>.Igniting hatred in order to cover it didn't work for him,because Cleo got under his skin,and found out that he is selfish and selfless,mean and kind,all at once.Cleo and Magnus feel so wrong due to their past but so right at the same time,I don't know when it happened but I ship them.Hard.He <i>will</i> do the right thing in the end.<b>I believe in him.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448445447ra/17141879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We both want to embrace who we are,we both want to stop being used by others and discarded at their will.We both desperately want control over our destinies,and revenge over our enemies.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Lucia my dear,your dream of being free of whoever tries to control you is fair,but you seriously need to consider visiting a therapist.He could help you with your anger management and your resentment towards everyone.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448445377ra/17141861.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Everything he touched turned to ash.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Except saving Lys,Jonas didn't make a single right choice.If it wasn't for Cleo guiding him,he would wander aimlessly in Paelsia reciting how much he wants a better future for his people.The way he handled things with Felix is one example of said weak choices.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440284260ra/15956821.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>December,you can't come fast enough.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/633529.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15604052310059258250" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

However one major one at the center of our disputes will be there and that is the one about who Cleo ends up with with.<br><a href="http://s1070.photobucket.com/user/SabrinaGreane/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/8310659_zps5c9ec359.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><b> Character Perspectives </b><br><u> Cleo </u> <br>Cleo wants to save Auranos from the rule of an evil king. She feels like a pawn, she wants to control her destiny and have her throne back, and she'll do whatever it takes.<br><u> Magnus </u><br>Magnus has been betrayed by everyone he loves, he feels lost and alone. However, he knows that Cleo is a greater threat to his father's kingdom than anyone knows, but Magnus has a secret, he is, too.<br><u> Lucia </u><br>Lucia is the one who is the key to finding the Kindred, she can take out an army alone, and she has attracted the attention of the Watchers. Alas, in Mytica you never know who you can trust, and who has other motives. Everyone has their own agenda, and Lucia's sick of them not caring about her, the one in the center of them all. <br><u> Alexius </u><br>Alexius is a Watcher who works for the one woman who could destroy him, Melanie. Melanie has given Alexius a daunting task he doesn't want to go through with, but Melanie has bound Alexius to her, and he is left without a choice. <br><u> Nic </u><br>Nic is Cleo's best friend, and the only family either of them has anymore. The palace is filled with people who hate Auranos, and those who are from it, given Nic a dangerous disadvantage. Not to mention, a mysterious prince who you don't know who's side he's on until the very end. <br><b> Plot </b><br><i> I am going to take important events from chapters and use a visual representation to explain what happens </i><br>Prologue<br>Prologues almost never make sense until the end, as this one did.<br><a href="http://s1070.photobucket.com/user/SabrinaGreane/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/ApRtCuz_zpsfda36316.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer362165457856383548"><i>Wh...Wha-t</i> have I just finished?! This book has completely changed the direction of the series. UNEXPECTEDLY AMAZING is just an understatement of what this book is. <br/> <br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/>=> Sabina is Magnus's REAL mother! I didn't like this. <br/><br/>=> Kindred, four elemental crystals which can give god-like powers to the keeper, have found! This is totally an unexpected thing I got from this book. I thought we would get them in the second last or last book. But NO!! Oh God! I am sooo excited right now! <br/><br/>=> Pr</span></span>
  <span id="freeText362165457856383548" style="display:none"><i>Wh...Wha-t</i> have I just finished?! This book has completely changed the direction of the series. UNEXPECTEDLY AMAZING is just an understatement of what this book is. <br /> <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />=&gt; Sabina is Magnus's REAL mother! I didn't like this. <br /><br />=&gt; Kindred, four elemental crystals which can give god-like powers to the keeper, have found! This is totally an unexpected thing I got from this book. I thought we would get them in the second last or last book. But NO!! Oh God! I am sooo excited right now! <br /><br />=&gt; Princess Amara. I didn't like her before in the series. I thought she was useless. At the same time I also had a speculation that she would must turn out to be useful. Because Morgan Rhodes doesn't like useless characters. Eventually I understood the role of Amara and pretty much liked it. She is blunt. Evil. Has craving for POWER. So far a good antagonist.<br /><br />=&gt; Felix was also an amazing addition. I liked him very much. I am very excited to read him more further in the series. <br /><br />=&gt; I am liking Jonas and Lysandra together. I humbly request to the author that PLEASE don't meddle with this!<br /><br />=&gt; I am liking how Magnus is improving. I am eager to read how he will face his father in the next book after what he has done.<br /><br />=&gt; King Gaius took the back seat here, didn't appear or act that much. So it was understandable that how this book was little less bloody. 😅<br /><br />=&gt; Kraeshia is now a threat for Mytica. Wow! King Gaius deserves to face this! <br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Overall, this book is a turning point in the series. And so far the best in the series.<br /><br />🌟🌟<b>4.5 Stars</b>🌟🌟<br /><br />July 8, 2017</span>

    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1898034424?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781595147066" href="/book/show/25065631-gathering-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1898034424" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer26401748392634188"><b>Update 3/14/2017:</b> I'm downgrading this to 4.5 stars. Comparing it to the previous two books, I think it's more appropriate for it to be a 4.5 instead of a full 5, which was my rating for the previous two books.<br/><br/><b>Original Review:</b><br/><br/><b>Basically, I'm in hell and I want out.</b> Did I sign up for this kind of pain? No (<s>Yes</s>). GUYS, I lost count of how many times I wanted to throw this book against a wall. <br/><br/>I originally wanted to give this 4.5 stars. I gave Falling Kingdoms and Rebel Spring both 5 stars, but with</span>
  <span id="freeText26401748392634188" style="display:none"><b>Update 3/14/2017:</b> I'm downgrading this to 4.5 stars. Comparing it to the previous two books, I think it's more appropriate for it to be a 4.5 instead of a full 5, which was my rating for the previous two books.<br /><br /><b>Original Review:</b><br /><br /><b>Basically, I'm in hell and I want out.</b> Did I sign up for this kind of pain? No (<s>Yes</s>). GUYS, I lost count of how many times I wanted to throw this book against a wall. <br /><br />I originally wanted to give this 4.5 stars. I gave Falling Kingdoms and Rebel Spring both 5 stars, but with Gathering Darkness, there was <i>something</i> lacking. Don't ask me what it is, because I'm not even sure what it is. I don't know. Yes, the book put me in misery and pain. Yes, it surprised me on countless occasions. Yes, I'm trash for the characters and the ships. Yes, I'm living for the plot. Yes, I binged it. <b>SOOOOOO</b>, I decided to ignore this <i>something</i> and rate the book a 5 because the book is perfect, let's be real. IF YOU HAVEN'T PICKED UP THE SERIES, WHAT ARE YOU WAITING FOR? DO IT.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“In the shadow my father has cast over my entire life, you are the only light I can see anymore. And, whatever the cost, I refuse to let that light be extinguished.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I still can't review this properly, I'll <i>try</i> to put effort into the characters section, because that's my favorite section. Just don't expect too much.<br /><br />The plot? Well, the plot is one big tangled web and basically, don't trust anyone. Also, nobody is safe. The random deaths are still there and I think this is the first time I feel overwhelmed by them. <br /><br />The characters? I'm trash for them, although I did want to smack some of them on the head. <br /><br />- Magnus is still my baby and <u>I adore him</u>, but he was an idiot this book, let's be real. I definitely do understand why he was acting the way he was, but still, LET MY SHIP SAIL. LET MAGNEO SAIL. HOW BEAUTIFUL IS THIS SHIP YOU GUYS????? I LIVE FOR MAGNEO. <br />- Jonas is still the same rebel leader with plans that go horribly wrong. There wasn't too many Jonas chapters in this book and weirdly I was... okay with it? I mean, don't get me wrong, I love him and all, but I just slightly lost interest in whatever he was going through. Why? I don't know. <br />- Lucia... oh Lucia. She's insane. Even more insane than in Rebel Spring. She's naive, too, but I completely understand that because she's 16 years old. Poor baby, she went through hell this book and I can't even begin to imagine how that will affect her in the next book. <br />- Now, Cleo, she's still pretty much the same. I love her, I love her determination to get her kingdom back. However, she didn't have any major development this book and that's fine because I don't see any room for that at that point.<br />- AND KING GAIUS, YOU PIECE OF SHIT, WHY AREN'T YOU DEAD YET?!?!?!<br />- Nic... oh Nic, you messed up so much in this book. BUT HE'S A POOR BABY TOO. THEY'RE ALL MY BABIES. Except the obvious shit characters. <br />- Lysandra, who was introduced in the previous book, also went through something really bad this book. Poor baby. I love how strong she is despite it all. However, we also didn't get many chapters for her as much as we did in Rebel Spring.<br />- Now, the Kraeshian (I can't even bother to check the spelling) siblings. I really liked Ashur, but Amara... GAH, I WANT TO KILL HER.<br />- This book also introduces a new character, Felix. I basically instantly loved him. I'm so excited to see more of his character!<br /><br />I don't know what else to say? <b>I just want to cry because I love this series so much?????</b> <br /><br /><u>Daily reminder from yours truly:</u> Read the books!</span>
  <a data-text-id="26401748392634188" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1660783921" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1660783921" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1660783921?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤  by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink">Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=my-favorite-covers">my-favorite-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=alternating-pov">alternating-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=trust-bone-recs">trust-bone-recs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=could-read-over-and-over-again">could-read-over-and-over-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1660783921" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12924094934915981046"><br/>*4.5 Stars*<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Cleo's cheeks flamed. "I hate you."<br/>"Good. You should never forget your place in this palace. You continue to live only because my father doesn't yet want you dead. You have no power here. And, most especially, <i>you have no power over me</i>." </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>It’s always extremely hard to talk about each book in a long series in a review, because you begin to spoil and become repetitive….but for Magnus?? I’d try just about anything. <b>This series</b>, while easily dismissed by those who aren’t truly enraptur</span>
  <span id="freeText12924094934915981046" style="display:none"><br>*4.5 Stars*<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Cleo's cheeks flamed. "I hate you."<br>"Good. You should never forget your place in this palace. You continue to live only because my father doesn't yet want you dead. You have no power here. And, most especially, <i>you have no power over me</i>." </blockquote>
</b><br><br>It’s always extremely hard to talk about each book in a long series in a review, because you begin to spoil and become repetitive….but for Magnus?? I’d try just about anything. <b>This series</b>, while easily dismissed by those who aren’t truly enraptured by one of the characters, <b>has a way of really getting under your skin</b>. It’s not so much the scenarios, though those are of some note as well, but about the characters and the deep-rooted connections you make with them.<br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/UQp0nN6_zpsehz3mdlx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424801970ra/13803815.gif" alt=" photo UQp0nN6_zpsehz3mdlx.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In all honesty, had I not connected immediately with Magnus, this series would have been discarded like many before. I am very busy, and I really only get to read around when I go to bed-about 10 PM, and then it’s right back to the 8-5 grind and I have to wait all over again. So, when I begin a book, series, <i>whatever</i>, I make sure it’s worth my time and that it touches my heart, one way or another. Some books touch me because of just their content (this is probably tribute to a couple years ago, more so than now) and <b>some reach me on a far deeper level than I could possibly imagine</b>....and that is because of the characters.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Magnus glanced at Cleo. She held her arms across the bodice of her rose-colored gown, which was far fancier than anything typically worn on a walk through a thick forest on a hot day. She regarded him with a silent, sour expression-not a new look for her by any means. <br>“And why are <i>you</i> here?” he asked her.<br>“I want to help,” she replied.<br>“Oh, yes. So helpful.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I never realized, until recently, how much my favorite books really center on the characters and their development. It's far more important to me now to have character-driven stories rather than all action and no character arcs. Sure, my absolute favorites are those that perfectly balance both story and people, but, lately, more often than not it’s all about if the characters reach me and touch my soul. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Some sought revenge against their mortal enemies with the edge of a sword. Her plan for vengeance began with the edge of a smile.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/giphy%2074_zpsrepwrazm.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465914781ra/19415875.gif" alt=" photo giphy 74_zpsrepwrazm.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And I’m not saying that action doesn’t pull me in….but it's definitely not my only drive anymore….and you can tell solely on my reviews that my preferences have changed. So, my point? This series, while action heavy and full of blood, destruction, mayhem, and peril, didn’t grip me for that reason. No, <b>this series gripped me on a far more addicting level</b>, and that honor solely belongs to my dear Magnus….and even Cleo.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/cruel-intentions-enemies-enemy-gif-kathryn-merteuil-Favim.com-290425_zpsln0yugcp.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465914781ra/19415876.gif" alt=" photo cruel-intentions-enemies-enemy-gif-kathryn-merteuil-Favim.com-290425_zpsln0yugcp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As the series has progressed, these two characters have obviously grown, interacted, and became the obsession of many a fangirl-me included-and now, here in book three, we are really getting deeper into their minds, and with that, my obsession is reaching an all-time high. And, frankly, the stories have became far more interesting.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I think that you hate your father. You hate him almost as much as I do.”<br>It took him a moment to realize he’d stopped breathing. “And what difference would it make if you’re right?” he finally managed.<br>“All the difference in the world.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br>And, let’s face it, our ship is finally sailing…or is it??? The other best part about this series? I, for once, <b>literally have no fucking clue what’s going to happen</b> and the sexual tension is DRIVING. ME. CRAZY. The twists and turns and admissions and deaths and ridiculous decisions…I swear, even halfway through book four, my head is still spinning. Stop it, Morgan Rhodes! Just…..STOP IT. Make it happen. <b>Fetch TOTALLY needs to happen</b>…PLEASE??<br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/giphy%2075_zpsi07qirnw.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465914781ra/19415877.gif" alt=" photo giphy 75_zpsi07qirnw.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>UGH. <br><br>So yeah, this isn’t a great review, but it’s not like anyone can read it if they haven’t read the series if I go all spoilery, so I chose to just…blabber. I miss blabbering. Blabbering about boys and books really does make me happy. So. Yeah. Take what you will from this nonsense…I’m off to work…and then tonight I’m hoping to FINALLY get what I want. I’m totally trusting Brittney, here. <b>She threw me a trust bone</b>, damn it. So I guess I’m supposed to sit here and wait and…trust. You know, until this alleged bone gets here. Ugh. <br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/8II6BKW_zpshpmxc4on.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465914781ra/19415878.gif" alt=" photo 8II6BKW_zpshpmxc4on.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea-peril-please-reviews/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287303i/17673713._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a title="Facebook" href="https://www.facebook.com/starcrossedbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055977i/15660595.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="Twitter" href="https://twitter.com/starcrossedblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055639i/15660580.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="RSS" href="http://feeds.feedburner.com/starcrossedbookblog/METU" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055639i/15660581.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="BLOGLOVIN" href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/star-crossed-book-blog-13035961" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055639i/15660579.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="Google+" href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/b/116866754719786372049/+Starcrossedbookblog/posts" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439651670i/15866819.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>****************<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Cleo's cheeks flamed. "I hate you."<br>"Good. You should never forget your place in this palace. You continue to live only because my father doesn't yet want you dead. You have no power here. And, most especially, <i>you have no power over me</i>." </blockquote>
</b><br><br>MY HEART.<br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/19366270_zpsdcyzoo8p.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465826107i/19405022.png" alt=" photo 19366270_zpsdcyzoo8p.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Need I say anything else? I mean...Magnus...<br><br>and <b>Magduck</b>! lolz<br><br>RTC.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12924094934915981046" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2147901292" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2147901292" />
    <a title="booksnpenguins" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66222749-booksnpenguins"><img alt="booksnpenguins" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580407796p2/66222749.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2147901292?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="booksnpenguins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="booksnpenguins" href="/user/show/66222749-booksnpenguins">booksnpenguins</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66222749-booksnpenguins?shelf=high-dark-epic-fantasy">high-dark-epic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66222749-booksnpenguins?shelf=period-aus-past">period-aus-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66222749-booksnpenguins?shelf=book-heaven">book-heaven</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66222749-booksnpenguins?shelf=shippity-ship-ship">shippity-ship-ship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66222749-booksnpenguins?shelf=royal-binches">royal-binches</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2147901292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3891719460972331930">Okay, I've got a question. <br/><a href='https://gifyu.com/image/M68h' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1507594938ra/24130427.gif' alt='tumblr_mtv5afZH6B1qili3vo3_500.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>How, in the name of all things sacred and holy <s>Magnus Lukas Damora included</s>, am I supposed to go to sleep after this? <br/>No, seriously, someone please answer me. <br/>I'm asking those who've read this book already, in particular. How did you menage to go on with your life after finishing this? Enlighten me, you selfish fools! <br/><br/>My head is a mess. My heart, empty and numb. My feels? All over the place. <br/>I've obviously just lost a duel against overwhelmingness and I have no ide</span>
  <span id="freeText3891719460972331930" style="display:none">Okay, I've got a question. <br><a href="https://gifyu.com/image/M68h" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1507594938ra/24130427.gif" alt="tumblr_mtv5afZH6B1qili3vo3_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>How, in the name of all things sacred and holy <s>Magnus Lukas Damora included</s>, am I supposed to go to sleep after this? <br>No, seriously, someone please answer me. <br>I'm asking those who've read this book already, in particular. How did you menage to go on with your life after finishing this? Enlighten me, you selfish fools! <br><br>My head is a mess. My heart, empty and numb. My feels? All over the place. <br>I've obviously just lost a duel against overwhelmingness and I have no idea what to do with myself, now. <br><br>I devoured this book. Read it in one sitting, again, like I did with Falling Kingdoms and Rebel Spring. I probably look like Bela Lugosi, now, bloodshot eyes, all pale and crinkled. <br>It left me weak and thirsty, panting and sweating. <br>Basically like sex, minus the happy ending, plus the angst. <br>Honestly, if I ran a marathon I probably wouldn't be this distressed. Now that I think about it twice, these two days filled with <s>the devil itself</s> Morgan Rhodes and her books, sort of felt like a marathon. Or a triathlon. I got no medal, though. Only a huge, slimy hole where my heart used to reside. <br>And to think I even had to pay for it! <br>I wasn't even halfway through it when shit started to go down and all I kept doing was turning pages and screaming. I'm pretty sure by now my neighbors think I've spent the night killing bears or doing karate in my living room, but the truth is that this book is the paper embodiment of <i>what the fuck</i> you wouldn't expect to love this much in a world already packed with mediocre WTFs. <br>And when it's like this, trust me, screaming comes natural. <br>This book is my favorite so far. <br>It has everything. Snarky plots and villain agendas. Infinitely frustrating but, <i>oh, so satisfying</i> character developments. Easily understandable and catchy writing. A couple of unnecessary love-drama attempts here and there for the sake of whatever. A few moments that made my insides squirm. Some good ol' stabby stab stab. Well portrayed examples of the destructive power of lies. Precarious family and friendship dynamics opposed to real feelings and emotions. A fair amount of heart-stopping moments that left me speechless and breathless. Romance-not-romance <s>because what else would you call this mess?</s>. <br>As I said, <b>everything</b>. <br>I'll never stop saying this: I am so glad I started this series. It owns me. It literally got me on fire, and I'm not even exaggerating.<br>I'll probably add something to this review, tomorrow, when my hands have stopped shaking and my brain isn't trying to escape my skull, anymore.<br>For now, let me just leave you with...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>This princess, who looked at him tonight with hope rather than hate shining in her eyes...if he let her, she could destroy him.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Intense, uh?<br>Now multiply this by infinity and you'll get a hint of how I feel like.<br>I'm dying. *cries in sarcasm* <b>Ain't that great?</b><br><br><br><b>the-day-after edit:</b> I survived. <br>Barely and not without a little pain, but I'm still here.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3891719460972331930" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1416994711" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1416994711" />
    <a title="Cody" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35007929-cody"><img alt="Cody" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415626292p2/35007929.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1416994711?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cody" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cody" href="/user/show/35007929-cody">Cody</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1416994711" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13800915495657178762">Gathering Darkness was without a doubt one of the best books I have read of 2016, <i>yes I know its January but still</i>. For those of you who have stumbled across my reviews on Falling Kingdoms and Rebel Spring, you will have noted that I really enjoyed the books but there was something missing, that initial spark or driving force being <b>liking</b> and <b>loving</b> a book. My feelings of Gathering Darkness- <b>I love this freaking book</b>. It's now one of my favourite series.<br/><br/>Falling Kingdoms and Rebel Spring are like</span>
  <span id="freeText13800915495657178762" style="display:none">Gathering Darkness was without a doubt one of the best books I have read of 2016, <i>yes I know its January but still</i>. For those of you who have stumbled across my reviews on Falling Kingdoms and Rebel Spring, you will have noted that I really enjoyed the books but there was something missing, that initial spark or driving force being <b>liking</b> and <b>loving</b> a book. My feelings of Gathering Darkness- <b>I love this freaking book</b>. It's now one of my favourite series.<br><br>Falling Kingdoms and Rebel Spring are like the stepping stones in the series, slowly preparing you for what’s to come, drawing you into this fantasy world full of love, betrayal and vengeance, which makes Gathering Darkness the book that dominates them all, leaving you a little breathless, in a state of shock and with a little trickle of fear that things are only just getting started. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Hatred is like fire. It burns the one who harnesses it. It’s also extremely hard to see more helpful truths through its flames.”</i>
</b><br><br>Gathering Darkness makes quick work of bringing you up to speed on the past events of the series and soon enough the plot is under way and your immersed once again in this ferocious magical world. Cleo, Jonas, Magnus and Lucia are locked and loaded in the this explosive sequel, better yet each is unrecognizable since book one, they continue to grow and change and not sometimes for the better but you can’t help but love them anyway, their journey is not one for the light hearted but their courage and commitment to their beliefs is contagious.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Some sought revenge against their mortal enemies with the edge of a sword. Her plan for vengeance began with the edge of a smile.”</i>
</b><br><br>I must commend yet again the multiple POV’s and how wonderfully entangled the writing is, you move smoothly from character to character and kingdom to kingdom but you don’t feel jolted and confused, everything is effortless. We also get to know the trickster Kraeshian sibling’s Prince Ashur and Princess Amara. Seemly innocent in the beginning but I assure you they have their own schemes and prove to be one of the biggest players in this ruthless game searching for the Kindred.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Fear and intimidation are tactics that work very well on those who allow themselves to be afraid and intimidated.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454011890ra/17904965.gif" width="350" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now I <b>must</b> talk about the romance, once more the romance <b>never</b> takes center stage but these mere snippets of moments are filled with such delicious tension, angst and smothering desire that I find myself developing the most <u>unhealthy</u> obsession with these characters and ships. I have fully jumped ship and I regret absolutely nothing, they are my life now, <s>so sad</s> and I will not be swayed.<br><br><b>
  <i>“It was desperate, this kiss. Violent, even.”</i>
</b><br><br>As I’ve said above this book was explosive, I mean fast-paced, full of action, don’t-you-dare-put-me-down-or-you’ll-miss-something-good, all consuming plot that makes the pages fly by. There were so many plot twists, shocking betrayals and although it pain’s me to even think of them but heartbreaking loses. I didn’t think Rhodes could be more brutal but again I’m in awe of her dark and bewitching skill to completely change a character that makes you-the reader throw away all those past opinions and feel a sense of kindred to them.<br><br><b>
  <i>“That is your greatest mistake. The love you felt for him wasn’t love at all—it was obsession. Real love means sacrifice, not selfishness.”</i>
</b><br><br>I may never recover from the cliffhanger, I’m actually telling people <b>“don’t read this book unless you have Frozen Tides within arms reach.”</b> And I stand by it. So many revelations come to light but it is not without sacrifice, I’m actually in complete denial about one aspect of the ending, I refuse to believe it, it’s cruel, devastating and just plain agony to think about. I currently have Frozen Tides within arms reach and it’s a battle every day to not tear my way through it like a possessed animal but the mere thought that Frozen Tides could end even half as badly as Gathering Darkness stills my too eager fingers because then I will be left waiting in agony for the next instalment and much-needed answers. I’ll eventually break down but I have some pretty epic books coming up on my TBR so I’ll stay strong, <b>for now</b>.<br><br>Gathering Darkness outshines its predecessors and shows a glimpse into just how giant and complex this world is and what exactly Rhodes has in store for her readers. You think you know the Kindred? You think you know what everyone is fighting for? <b>Think again!</b><br><br><a href="http://literary-lyobsessed.blogspot.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Literary-ly Obsessed (Blog)</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/CodyLeighDuffy" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/codyleighduffy/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="13800915495657178762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16428289959998667640">If you would all be as Kind as to excuse me while I scream from having my mind blown that would be greatly appreciated. <br/> <br/> Why is my mind blown? Because this series has officially become one of my absolute favorites. And it's because of what a wild ride this book was. Full of numerous deaths and revelations, this was by all means the definition of epic. <br/><br/> Morgan Rhodes really knows how to make your heart pound and making you lose your mind. This world, it's insane. I can't say much about the plot </span>
  <span id="freeText16428289959998667640" style="display:none">If you would all be as Kind as to excuse me while I scream from having my mind blown that would be greatly appreciated. <br /> <br /> Why is my mind blown? Because this series has officially become one of my absolute favorites. And it's because of what a wild ride this book was. Full of numerous deaths and revelations, this was by all means the definition of epic. <br /><br /> Morgan Rhodes really knows how to make your heart pound and making you lose your mind. This world, it's insane. I can't say much about the plot due to spoilers, but holy hell was it epic. <br /> <br /> "In the shadow my father has cast over my entire life, you are the only light I can see anymore. And, whatever the cost, I refuse to let that light extinguish." <br /> MY SHIP FINALLY STARTED SAILING. MAGNEO HAS STARTED SAILING. <br />Jesus the amount of times I swooned, cried and just burst out of pure joy was ridiculous. I loved the development of the growing romance between Magnus and Cleo. It was EVERYTHING I've ever wanted in an epic fantasy. <br /> All the secrets, twists and betrayals were unbelievable. Why kill off one character when you can kill off everyone just when I start to care for them, the more the merrier, right??? <br />God this was perfection. My absolute favorite in the series so far, and I don't think I can wait a week for Frozen Tides because THAT ENDING. HOLY FIRE GOD. WHY CAN'T THESE BOOKS BE LONGER. I NEVER WANT THEM TO END.</span>

<div id="review_644296958" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/644296958" />
    <a title="Jackie Chapman" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7040977-jackie-chapman"><img alt="Jackie Chapman" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1342238076p2/7040977.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/644296958?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jackie Chapman" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jackie Chapman" href="/user/show/7040977-jackie-chapman">Jackie Chapman</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781595147059" href="/book/show/20821149-gathering-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7040977-jackie-chapman?shelf=2014-must-reads">2014-must-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7040977-jackie-chapman?shelf=gimme-sequels">gimme-sequels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7040977-jackie-chapman?shelf=third-in-a-series">third-in-a-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer644296958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11996680375680363088"><b>UPDATE: Dec. 10, 2014<br/>MAY CONTAIN SPOILERS FOR GD</b><br/>Right off the bat, I LOVED this book! I read it within a 24 hour period, which is huge for me since my other anticipated reads usually take me about 2-3 days to finish. But I just devoured this book and although short-lived I loved every minute of it. GD definitely does not disappoint. Even after I was done with it I found myself rereading my favorite passages. Right from the beginning of this book down to the last page everything was on higher sta</span>
  <span id="freeText11996680375680363088" style="display:none"><b>UPDATE: Dec. 10, 2014<br>MAY CONTAIN SPOILERS FOR GD</b><br>Right off the bat, I LOVED this book! I read it within a 24 hour period, which is huge for me since my other anticipated reads usually take me about 2-3 days to finish. But I just devoured this book and although short-lived I loved every minute of it. GD definitely does not disappoint. Even after I was done with it I found myself rereading my favorite passages. Right from the beginning of this book down to the last page everything was on higher stakes and you could simply feel the tension resonating all throughout the book. I have to admit that in the beginning it did have a slow start but a few chapters in and I was hooked once again into this exhilarating world. I thoroughly enjoyed going back to this world that Morgan has created and reuniting with all of my favorite characters. Everything essentially picks up right where RS had left off and I loved that there were no big time gaps in this book and we're plucked back into the world. There were so many twists in this book that had me gasping to downright giggling. Some of my favorite passages in this book were (you guessed it;)) the scenes with Cleo and Magnus. Their banter and hate for each other had me smiling through their scenes together. You can definitely see through each of their facades that they both harbor feelings for each other that neither of them will admit, not even to themselves.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[but through the end of the book Magnus finally comes to a realization that he's got it bad for Cleo (hehe) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I would think that their relationship would have progressed by the end of GD, but I kind of like that Morgan Rhodes really takes her time with their scenes together that will culminate into a slow-burn romance (which is my favorite kind of romance). With each scene they have together Cleo is able to peel back layers of Magnus and manages to get him to let his guard go down when he's around her. However, I'm still wary of Magnus' romantic feelings for Lucia. Yes, he still cares deeply for Lucia, but we can also see that Lucia no longer visits his dreams anymore either. We can see that there's this rift that is forming between them. And Magnus can also see that Lucia is not the only one that doesn't see him as a monster or just a replica of his father, King Gaius. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I love the quote that Magnus says to Cleo: "...without your bravery in the face of all that's happened to you, without your constant scheming behind my back, without that fire of hatred and contempt and <i>hope</i> in your eyes when you look at me...In the shadow my father has cast over my entire life, you are the only light I can see anymore. And, whatever the cost, I refuse to let that light be extinguished. (p.345)" This quote was just simply heartbreaking (Oh, Magnus, you poor thing...)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> No matter how civil they try to act to one another they always end up in a heated argument, which feeds into their sexual frustrations for each other. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[check out page 346 *wink* *wink* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I just can't wait where their relationship goes from here. After the events that took place in GD, there has definitely been a reduction on the love web. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>(1) Magnus and Cleo are still strong (Magnus admits to himself that he's fallen in love with Cleo)<br>(2) Magnus still harbors feelings for Lucia, Lucia still doesn't return them<br>(3) Jonas still has strong feelings for Cleo and Cleo may return his affections<br>(4) Lysandra and Jonas are both head over heals for each other<br>(5) Alexius and Lucia are done-zo since Alexius is dead<br>(6) Nic and Ashur is over before it even started since Ashur is dead<br>(7) Nic may not be as in love with Cleo as he once did<br>(8) Amara was just toying with Magnus for her own personal agenda <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I love that Morgan utilizes her characters as pawns on a chess game because she has her pieces scattered everywhere. And I love that you don't really know what move is going to happen next. Even the ending (which btw ends in a cliffhanger) caught me by surprise that I'm not really sure where the rest of the series is headed. Overall, GD was a fantastic sequel that did not disappoint!<br><b>UPDATE: Dec. 5, 2014<br>LOOK AT THIS PROMOTIONAL PIC FOR GATHERING DARKNESS I FOUND ON MORGAN'S TWITTER!!</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417834783i/12556716._SY540_.jpg" width="650" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>THERE ARE A LOT OF SUSPICIONS THAT THESE ARE MAGNUS AND CLEO</b><br>Just the past couple of weeks Morgan has dropped so many clues about these two:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417837480i/12557538.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417837480i/12557539.jpg" width="550" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417837631i/12557576.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417837631i/12557577.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417837777i/12557601._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417837777i/12557602.jpg" width="650" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417839996i/12558253._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417839996i/12558254._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417840163i/12558357._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417840163i/12558358._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417840262i/12558423.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>End of Update</b><br><br>{{This review contains spoilers for FK and RS. This is pretty much just me ranting about the romance that was set up in RS}} After I read Falling Kingdoms I was so sure that Cleo and Jonas would hook up. And I never really considered Magnus as a prospect for Cleo romantically. But I slowly found myself liking Magnus more in Rebel Spring, and I really seemed to enjoy the scenes in which Cleo and Magnus are bickering. I wouldn't mind if they do end up together and they seem to be brushing off on each other. I found it pretty cute when the other would start defending the other about their motives (i.e. Magnus defending Cleo's honor and Cleo defending Magnus to Nic after the assassination attempt). And out of the two guys that Cleo locks lips with in Rebel Spring I found her kiss with Magnus a lot steamier. Even though their marriage was not of their own accord I think that their marriage has forced them to bond and I think as of the moment they really need each other to balance the other out. Their romance resembles that of Beauty and the Beast in which Cleo tries to seek out the real Magnus underneath the facade to be the perfect son to his father; several times Magnus and Cleo bicker about whether or not he even has a heart, and I found this parallel very endearing.<br><br>Though the romance in this novel seems to be all over the place, just the number of guys who are interested in Cleo is astounding: Theon, Aron, Nic, Jonas, and Magnus. I mean I know she is described as this "golden princess," but all of these guys are just falling for her right and left. <br><br>I found that some of the romantic revelations that went on in Rebel Spring solved some of the issues with some the characters like having Magnus marry Cleo would solve the Magnus-having-feelings-for-his-sister problem and Lucia having a thing for Alexius would relieve some of the weirdness going on between her and Magnus and having Nic suddenly become the LGBT character in the series knocks him off as a potential love interest for Cleo (even though Theon and Aron were also killed off in order to knock them out of the running as well). <br><br>And another thing...I would root for Cleo and Jonas if there weren't so many obstacles like Cleo's marriage to Magnus (that's kind of a big hurtle to get through and I don't think the concept of divorce even existed let alone an option and I doubt the author would kill him off, at least not until the last book in the series) and her status as the last heir to her kingdom and the fact that she has obligations to her people and Jonas is not even of royal blood to consider him for a long-term relationship for someone who is now a queen in her own right.<br><br>Overall, after reading Rebel Spring all of my emotions are kind of jumbled, but as of right now I am really rooting for Magnus and Cleo to make it through to the end! &lt;3</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10675488-swaye?shelf=2018">2018</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2316341833" class="readable"
