<span id="freeTextContainer6085032118576129883">This book left me feeling seriously conflicted.<br/><br/>To be honest, there were huge chunks of it I simply didn't enjoy and it felt more like a chore than anything remotely resembling pleasure to get through. Most of the story felt like it was going around in circles and every chapter often just repeated the same sentiments over and over again from each character's POV. <br/><br/>Personally, there is nothing more frustrating in a series than when an author feels the need to recap what happened in the previous boo</span>
  <span id="freeText6085032118576129883" style="display:none">This book left me feeling seriously conflicted.<br /><br />To be honest, there were huge chunks of it I simply didn't enjoy and it felt more like a chore than anything remotely resembling pleasure to get through. Most of the story felt like it was going around in circles and every chapter often just repeated the same sentiments over and over again from each character's POV. <br /><br />Personally, there is nothing more frustrating in a series than when an author feels the need to recap what happened in the previous books. What sane individual is going to pick up the 3rd book in a series and read it as a standalone? I feel like it's lazy storytelling and a complete waste of time. For me, a lot of Gathering Darkness felt like a desperate need to reach a word count instead of focusing on plot progression and there were many times when I felt a compelling urge to throw the book out the window. <b>ESPECIALLY</b> when it came to Jonas' chapters. Holy chicken nugget in a biscuit dipped in mashed potato! What an incredibly pointless and annoying character! He, <i>by far</i>, wins all the awards for the horndoggiest character ever written. He goes from lusting after one character to another and then even pervs a fucking statue ffs! The man is incorrigible!<br /><br />Now that I've got all of that out of my system, I have to say that the ending of this book was so bloody brilliant that I very nearly gave it a 4 star rating. But alas, overall, I just felt like the book waffled way too much until it finally got there. <br /><br />I was going to take a break before beginning Frozen Tides but I NEED MORE MAGNEO IN MY LIFE!!! That, and my bae, Lucia is on the cover. *sigh* My poor, beautiful sorceress. I just want her to be happy. IS THAT TOO MUCH TO ASK, MORGAN RHODES, YOU MAGNIFICENT BUT MERCILESS MURDERER OF DARLINGS!?</span>
  <a data-text-id="6085032118576129883" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5703217548034612890" style="display:none">Buddy read with Diana Bautista!!! <br><br><i>"Darkness rose up to cover him like a thick cloak. Soon he’d make them all burn for what they’d done to him."</i><br><br>This was a fun read, definitely better than the second book! I want to start the fourth one right now, but the 5th book doesn't come out till December!! Must wait a few months. :(<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464555214i/19250809.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3009983930" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2084251709424291596"><b>4.5 Golden Stars</b><br/><br/>it's my least favourite in this series (the plot was more talking than actions) but I'm struggling to give it 5 stars or not.<br/>It had many Beautiful moments (especially after chapter 17! *heart eyes*) or Exciting, Mysterious when they tried to cross each other, Funny when it was the sarcastic arguing; as you noticed, I updated my progress very often, because I wanted to manifest my feelings! (or I would explode! no kidding!)<br/>many Mind-Blowing situations! & the Climax!<br/>I laughed, I sm</span>
  <span id="freeText2084251709424291596" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Golden Stars</b><br /><br />it's my least favourite in this series (the plot was more talking than actions) but I'm struggling to give it 5 stars or not.<br />It had many Beautiful moments (especially after chapter 17! *heart eyes*) or Exciting, Mysterious when they tried to cross each other, Funny when it was the sarcastic arguing; as you noticed, I updated my progress very often, because I wanted to manifest my feelings! (or I would explode! no kidding!)<br />many Mind-Blowing situations! &amp; the Climax!<br />I laughed, I smirked (at sarcastic comments), I shouted internally! (at the stupidity of my fav characters!) I cried, I screeched! (because of my ships) I swore a few times &amp; there was heart in my eyes! I was startled &amp; thrilled! I screamed (internally), I could've fallen of my seat out of too much anticipation! &amp; had all kinds of emotions.<br /><br />Magnus, Prince of Sass, charming as always.<br />&amp; his chapters were the most fascinating ones.<br /><br />This book had many revelations &amp; twists.<br />I found two absolute ships in this book.<br />Magnus, Jonas, Felix, Ashur, Nic, Alexius; characters I cared &amp; liked.<br />each Cleo, Lucia or Lysandra had moments when I hated them, but there were moments I liked them too (sinus-like interest); Between them, I think Lysandra was the best, &amp; <s>Cleo had a good character development, I hated her at book one, now I admire her. (since the middle of the book, it stayed this way, let's see how long it lasts.)</s><br /><br />the world is gray; anyone would manipulate the others to achieve their own goals, each character I believe as good ones did make mistakes, but still all of them are interesting. the power play &amp; politics in this story is very intriguing.<br />-<br />World building: ★★★★/5<br />Characters: ★★★★★/5<br />Writing style: ★★★★/5<br />Plot: ★★★★/5<br />General idea: ★★★★★/5</span>

        <a title="Caitlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin">Caitlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=2017-rereads">2017-rereads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=2017-read">2017-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1800698766" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11629083965583911070">I was talking to some of my friends at about the half way point of this book and I was complaining because so far the first 2 books were only 4 stars and this one was also looking like being a 4 star. However, the last 200 pages completely changed my opinion because it was ridiculously intense. I was on the edge of my seat reading it and I had to take breaks because I was so stressed. I was pretty sure that our main characters would survive this book but I was still extremely worried that someon</span>
  <span id="freeText11629083965583911070" style="display:none">I was talking to some of my friends at about the half way point of this book and I was complaining because so far the first 2 books were only 4 stars and this one was also looking like being a 4 star. However, the last 200 pages completely changed my opinion because it was ridiculously intense. I was on the edge of my seat reading it and I had to take breaks because I was so stressed. I was pretty sure that our main characters would survive this book but I was still extremely worried that someone was going to (literally) lose their head. <br /><br />I was set on taking a break between book 2 and 3 but I was too addicted to the story to leave the world just yet. I almost fell into a slump because of it so I had to read a quick trashy novel to deal with it. Even though this book ended on a type of cliffhanger (nothing was really resolved), I'll still be taking a tiny break from the world.<br /><br />Even though I finished this book last night I can't even remember half of the plot. It was so intense though and I was genuinely concerned for the safety of my favourites. So many twists shocked me (I actually sent videos to my friends of me screaming at how shocked I was). <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Such as Magnus' mum being Sabina, Nik and Ashur working together, Magnus saving Cleo, etc.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />The thing that changed this book from a 4 star to a 5 star were the <b>SHIPS</b> (don't read this section if you don't want to find out the ships)<br /><br />Magnus and Cleo are my 2 favourites characters and the fact that they're a ship makes me insanely happy. I love them so much. There's literally nothing better than an enemies turned to lovers. <br /><br /><i>"In the shadow my father has cast over my entire life, you are the only light I can see anymore. And, whatever the cost, I refuse to let that light be extinguished." </i> <br /><br />Literally this quote made me melt. This was followed by Cleo telling Magnus she hates him and then they started making out and omg my heart was about to explode. I just love it so much!<br /><br />Jonas and Lysandra was also a really cute new ship that I was totally rooting for since book 2. Their sneaky little kiss was so cute and I hope we get more of them.<br /><br />Poor little Lucia <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[got her heart broken by Alexius  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and I felt so bad for her when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he died <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />I love this series so much and I'm 200% addicted!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11629083965583911070" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4735109092961769264"><u>3.75 The stakes have never been higher. ★'s</u> <br/><br/><b>“There are no guarantees in this life, only strong possibilities. That's enough for me.” </b><br/><br/><i>“You don't cry when someone pushes you down. You get up. You get up and you fight back. And pretty soon nobody's going to shove you anymore because they'll see it's not worth it.” </i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1522711566i/25313909._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> Okay... So I gotta say, I still didn't love it! But at least "Gathering Darkness" was better than <i>Rebel Spring</i> even if only by a little bit. My biggest problem with this series is the re</span>
  <span id="freeText4735109092961769264" style="display:none"><u>3.75 The stakes have never been higher. ★'s</u> <br><br><b>“There are no guarantees in this life, only strong possibilities. That's enough for me.” </b><br><br><i>“You don't cry when someone pushes you down. You get up. You get up and you fight back. And pretty soon nobody's going to shove you anymore because they'll see it's not worth it.” </i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1522711566i/25313909._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> Okay... So I gotta say, I still didn't love it! But at least "Gathering Darkness" was better than <i>Rebel Spring</i> even if only by a little bit. My biggest problem with this series is the relationships. Especially the new relationship between <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Cleo and Magnus <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, though I seen it coming from a mile away! I have a hard time believing in the relationships. I honestly doubt any of these characters even know what real love is! Seeing as how the word LOVE gets tossed around more often than not. As I have said before, these said feelings come out of nowhere. One moment everything is normal than <b>BAM</b> feelings blossom out of thin air. It just really annoys me because one of my favorite things about reading is getting to see love grow and become strong. Getting to see two people grow together and become who they were always meant to be but this series does not give me this pleasure :( The fault of this disconnect for me could be that the characters spend way to much time alone and not enough time with each other. They don't really get the chance to actually bond and to truly get to know one another. Plus its all pretty predictable! I felt that this book was a lot slower but towards the middle/end is where it finally started picking up speed and become more interesting. I also really don't like Jonas being the <i>"rebel leader"</i>. I mean c'mon it's laughable at best. He really doesn't do much rebelling and when he does people die!! ¯\_(ツ)_/¯ Despite this <b>↑↑↑</b> it was still an enjoyable read for the most part. I do still like the world and the plot. I love my girl Cleo! She is my favorite character :D Shes like the only one, I can say that I FEEL I truly know. I wish it was from her POV more often than any of the others. In this installment there is a lot of death, betrayals, twists and turns, new friends/new enemies and even more death. Who can be trusted? Where do your loyalties lie? Mine have been and will always remain with Princess Cleo ;) <br><br><b>*This cover though, it's really something pretty*</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1522711566i/25313909._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“It was desperate, this kiss. Violent, even.<br>But of course it was. It had been building up between them for such a long time, as the battle about this boy who had destroyed her life had raged inside her. This boy who had saved her life, who was cruel and kind, strong and weak. Who was selfish and selfless all at once.” </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1523171281ra/25343048.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Magnus had come to a horrible realization. One that he knew would cause him nothing but pain and suffering from that day forward.<br>But there was no changing the truth of it.<br>He had fallen in love with her.”</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText7573107313720265255" style="display:none">Just finished Book 3 in the Pushy Librarian series, and it was AWESOME!<br>How did I not know about this series before a month ago?!<br><i>I'm guessing it was because Pushy Librarian wasn't quite pushy enough.</i><br>Anyway, this is a <i>reallyreallyreally</i> good mature young adult fantasy.     <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19673751-elena?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer826368451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13686408005895015101"><b>''And in this moment, he thought she was the bravest and most beautiful girl he'd ever known.''</b><br/><br/>Not going to lie here...I'M SO FREAKIN HAPPY RIGHT NOW!<br/>I mean I'm devastated at the same time because I have to wait a whole year for the next one. And then another year. And then...another one. This is awful. BUT I'm still thoroughly happy, because, guess what? My ship is finally sailing and I'm so excited to see how everything continues in the next installment!<br/><br/>I'm not going to say anything about the </span>
  <span id="freeText13686408005895015101" style="display:none"><b>''And in this moment, he thought she was the bravest and most beautiful girl he'd ever known.''</b><br /><br />Not going to lie here...I'M SO FREAKIN HAPPY RIGHT NOW!<br />I mean I'm devastated at the same time because I have to wait a whole year for the next one. And then another year. And then...another one. This is awful. BUT I'm still thoroughly happy, because, guess what? My ship is finally sailing and I'm so excited to see how everything continues in the next installment!<br /><br />I'm not going to say anything about the plot, because it is the third one, just know: <br /><br />1. If you loved the first two books in the series, you are going to love this just as much and if not than even more!<br />2. If you're not sure whether to start this series or not, then please just do it!<br /><br />This book follows a bunch of different characters, some of these I hate/dislike and some of these I simply ADORE! <br />Magnus is by far my favourite character. He is complex in so many ways. A pained and moody guy, who from time to time shows that he actually has a heart. There is nothing more I could ask for in a male character. <br />When it comes to the female characters Cleo is the one I can relate to the most. She has a weak side but is so strongheaded and keen at the same time. This is something I absolutely love about her! She doesn't have to be a killing machine to actually be badass. <br />Even though there are so many characters in this series I love, Jonas for instance, I have to say that I always founnd myself wanting to read about Cleo and Magnus. I just needed more of them!<br /><br />As for characters I disliked....not going to say much about them, but Lucia and Alexius just pissed me off.<br />Knew each other for 2 hours and confessed their love. Irgh. <br /><br /><b>''In the shadow my father has cast over my entire life, you are the only light I can see anymore.''</b><br /><br />This series is so addicting and unputdownable! I can't wait to lay my hands on the next installment! </span>
  <a data-text-id="13686408005895015101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9204518408958377200">Rating - 4/4.5 stars ✨ <br/><br/>In conclusion, I can’t fucking deal with this anymore. <br/>You know when something hurts, but it's just so good, you'll gladly take the pain?<br/>That’s slow burn romance and basically the entire Falling Kingdoms series for you all. <br/><br/>(spoilers ahead for the rest of the book)<br/><br/>I LOVE MAGNUS LUKAS DAMORA. With all my heart. He is the most cruel, bitter, and loving boy to ever exist and I LOVE HIM. his character is so complex and villainous but I just love him. <br/><br/>in fact I love him so much</span>
  <span id="freeText9204518408958377200" style="display:none">Rating - 4/4.5 stars ✨ <br /><br />In conclusion, I can’t fucking deal with this anymore. <br />You know when something hurts, but it's just so good, you'll gladly take the pain?<br />That’s slow burn romance and basically the entire Falling Kingdoms series for you all. <br /><br />(spoilers ahead for the rest of the book)<br /><br />I LOVE MAGNUS LUKAS DAMORA. With all my heart. He is the most cruel, bitter, and loving boy to ever exist and I LOVE HIM. his character is so complex and villainous but I just love him. <br /><br />in fact I love him so much, if you're going to have him kill his father’s most trusted guard just to save the girl he loves, I’m not gonna have any bad feelings towards him. (also, that was the plot twist of the century, still shaking a little)<br /><br />but- this is slow burn, and it’s not the easy, paved road that you expect. it’s a bumpy one.<br />so, I hate Amara. like what a manipulative snake and bitch. die. I feel unsafe that she has one of the Kindred. <br />Also, Felix was a manwhore. “Girls only belong in the kitchen, what else does that mouth do?” OH GOD. what an ass. but I did feel pretty bad for him, eventually. AND HE HAS A KINDRED. HOW MANY ARE GOING AROUND IN THE HANDS OF LITERALLY EVERYONE. <br />i seriously could give 2 shits about Lucia and Alexius because you guys had an instalove which I don’t appreciate. doesn't look good against the backdrop of magneo and an amazing slow-burn. <br />Jonas is just as fucking bipolar as ever. One minute he’s thinking about the princess, the next he’s kissing Lysandra? You okay? <br />Dear Nic; I’M SORRY I HATED YOU. you ain’t that bad. But you did not have to spill the beans to Amara about literally everything. <br /><br /><br />Seriously, I just need Magneo and that’s it. The need is surreal. <br />But the fantasy is building and building, deaths are happening in the blink of an eye, one villain dies, another appears, and Morgan’s a genius no matter what. <br />GIMME REBEL SPRING <br /><br /></span>

<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_7801229'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7801229-the-exiled-queen"><img alt="The Exiled Queen (Seven Realms, #2)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1285276245l/7801229._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('B94625OYiq65bYxqh6WpVycyDUbIyaE6NFjGSD3eGBD6uRs+7rBt7gemtCMmJbj7aTeQdrjcnSZ1vN6Nvbm+6Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kv+wctNEdw3Jp6Q5emcIKVId4Q+L9CZeRwjyDrp8HD9vmJGXrmyQTXdsnHDb5xmFHBh8P/vhGkIG7OrLOhu6xg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer16339852762692483757">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet vor</span>
  <span id="freeText16339852762692483757" style="display:none">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet voracious reader of all kinds of books. Under another pen name, she’s a national bestselling author of many paranormal novels. Falling Kingdoms is her first high fantasy. </span>

            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class='navButtonArrow sliderArrowPrev'></div>
</div>
